Introduction

This api documentation included mobile api, admin dashboard api

Base URL: https://myayasompo.ayasompo.com

This documentation aims to provide all the information you need to work with our API.

As you scroll, you'll see code examples for working with the API in different programming languages in the dark area to the right (or as part of the content on mobile). You can switch the language used with the tabs at the top right (or from the nav menu at the top left on mobile).

Authenticating requests

This API is not authenticated.

Endpoints

GET api/app/v1/products

Example request:
curl --request GET \
    --get "https://myayasompo.ayasompo.com/api/app/v1/products" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "https://myayasompo.ayasompo.com/api/app/v1/products"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());

Example response (200):

Show headers 
cache-control: no-cache, private
content-type: application/json
x-ratelimit-limit: 60
x-ratelimit-remaining: 59
access-control-allow-origin: *

POST api/app/v1/customer/is-exist

Example request:

    "https://myayasompo.ayasompo.com/api/app/v1/customer/is-exist " \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"phone\": \"dolorem\"
}"

    "https://myayasompo.ayasompo.com/api/app/v1/customer/is-exist "
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

    "phone": "dolorem"
};

    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());

POST api/admin/v1/customer/{id}

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "https://myayasompo.ayasompo.com/api/admin/v1/customer/97" \
    --header "Content-Type: multipart/form-data" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --form "is_disabled=356509.02955281"\
    --form "user_id=8789"\
    --form "customer_code=harum"\
    --form "customer_phoneno=qui"\
    --form "user_name=quasi"\
    --form "app_customer_type=INDIVIDUAL"\
    --form "risk_seqNo=et"\
    --form "risk_name=dolorum"\
    --form "policy_number=delectus"\
    --form "profile_photo=@/tmp/php52pHE9" 
const url = new URL(
    "https://myayasompo.ayasompo.com/api/admin/v1/customer/97"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "multipart/form-data",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

const body = new FormData();
body.append('is_disabled', '356509.02955281');
body.append('user_id', '8789');
body.append('customer_code', 'harum');
body.append('customer_phoneno', 'qui');
body.append('user_name', 'quasi');
body.append('app_customer_type', 'INDIVIDUAL');
body.append('risk_seqNo', 'et');
body.append('risk_name', 'dolorum');
body.append('policy_number', 'delectus');
body.append('profile_photo', document.querySelector('input[name="profile_photo"]').files[0]);

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body,
}).then(response => response.json());
Received response:
Request failed with error:


Tip: Check that you're properly connected to the network.
If you're a maintainer of ths API, verify that your API is running and you've enabled CORS.
You can check the Dev Tools console for debugging information.

    "https://myayasompo.ayasompo.com/api/admin/v1/customer/agent/deleniti" \

    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"expired_date\": \"2024-10-28T15:48:38\"
}"

const url = new URL(
    "https://myayasompo.ayasompo.com/api/admin/v1/customer/agent/deleniti"
);

    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "expired_date": "2024-10-28T15:48:38"
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "PUT",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());

POST api/admin/v1/messaging

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "https://myayasompo.ayasompo.com/api/admin/v1/messaging" \
    --header "Content-Type: multipart/form-data" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --form "title=tempore"\
    --form "message=quis"\
    --form "type=Broadcast"\
    --form "description=Aut aut libero animi vel perspiciatis."\
    --form "noti_for=Promotions"\
    --form "customers=quia"\
    --form "image_url=@/tmp/phphP5vzM" 
const url = new URL(
    "https://myayasompo.ayasompo.com/api/admin/v1/messaging"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "multipart/form-data",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

const body = new FormData();
body.append('title', 'tempore');
body.append('message', 'quis');
body.append('type', 'Broadcast');
body.append('description', 'Aut aut libero animi vel perspiciatis.');
body.append('noti_for', 'Promotions');
body.append('customers', 'quia');
body.append('image_url', document.querySelector('input[name="image_url"]').files[0]);

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body,
}).then(response => response.json());
Received response:
Request failed with error:


Tip: Check that you're properly connected to the network.
If you're a maintainer of ths API, verify that your API is running and you've enabled CORS.
You can check the Dev Tools console for debugging information.

Example: tempore

    --header "Accept: application/json"

);

    "Content-Type": "application/json",

};

    method: "DELETE",

}).then(response => response.json());

POST api/admin/v1/reset-password/customer

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "https://myayasompo.ayasompo.com/api/admin/v1/reset-password/customer" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"customer_id\": \"6832\"
}"

const url = new URL(
    "https://myayasompo.ayasompo.com/api/admin/v1/reset-password/customer"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "customer_id": "6832"
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());
Received response:
Request failed with error:


Tip: Check that you're properly connected to the network.
If you're a maintainer of ths API, verify that your API is running and you've enabled CORS.
You can check the Dev Tools console for debugging information.

POST api/admin/v1/reset-password/customer/{id}/send-sms

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "https://myayasompo.ayasompo.com/api/admin/v1/reset-password/customer/97/send-sms" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "https://myayasompo.ayasompo.com/api/admin/v1/reset-password/customer/97/send-sms"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());
